- Add support for multiple programming languages in problem solutions
  ([`5542a7b`](https://github.com/QuBenhao/LeetCode/commit/5542a7bde7f4e0586381567b79ef711ee1cb9589))

The scripts have been updated to support fetching of problem solutions in multiple languages. The
  "get_problem" script includes a new parameter "languages" and now is able to process and write
  solutions for both Python and Golang. Also, "daily_auto" and "daily_submission" scripts will now
  default to Python3 in case of an invalid or missing LANGUAGES environment variable.

- Refactor TreeNode conversion methods and add tests
  ([`537ab68`](https://github.com/QuBenhao/LeetCode/commit/537ab68431f0e90bb08f36b4039508bce16efa16))

The code refactors the way TreeNodes are converted to arrays and vice versa in Golang. It removes
  old commented Python code and introduces new, tested Golang functions for converting an array to a
  TreeNode, an array to a TreeNode with a target, and a TreeNode back to an array. Also, new test
  cases are added to ensure the correctness of these functions.
